The BMW M5 is a high-performance variant of the BMW 5 Series marketed under the BMW Msub-brand. It is considered an iconic vehicle in the sports sedan category. The M5 has always been produced in the sedan (saloon) body style, but in some countries the M5 has also been available as a wagon (estate) from 1992 to 1995, from 2006 to 2010, and since 2024. The first M5 model was hand-built in 1985 on the E28 535i chassis with a modified engine from the M1 that made it the fastest production sedan at the time. M5 models have been produced for every generation of the 5 Series since 1985.

Design and Aerodynamics: The GT-R R35 features a sleek, aggressive design with functional aerodynamics to enhance performance. It has a distinctive front grille, sharp lines, and a rear spoiler to improve downforce. All-Wheel Drive System: The GT-R uses Nissan's ATTESA E-TS all-wheel-drive system, which provides exceptional grip and stability, especially in challenging driving conditions. Advanced Technology: The GT-R is equipped with a sophisticated multi-function display that provides various performance metrics. It includes advanced electronics such as the Vehicle Dynamic Control (VDC) system. Interior: The interior combines luxury with functionality, featuring high-quality materials, supportive seats, and a driver-focused layout. It includes modern amenities such as a touchscreen infotainment system, premium audio system, and navigation. Hugs are way above physical interaction they are bridge between souls, where words dissolve and only pure, unspoken love remains. I feel when you hug someone you find the essence of another’s existence, their hopes, fears, and everything in between. It’s the purest form of human connection, a gesture that says, “I see you, I feel you, and I’m here for you.” Hugs should be normalized because they are the threads that weave us together, They remind us that we are not alone, that amidst the complexities of life, there is always a place where our hearts can rest. To normalize hugs is to acknowledge our need for closeness, for the reassurance that someone else’s heartbeat is in sync with ours, even if only for a few precious seconds. It’s a gentle reminder that in a world often harsh and fragmented, there are still simple, tender gestures that can heal and unite us. #hugs #selflove #validation #validateyourself #selfcare #positivity #gesture

Pls read the caption 👇 . **Title: Embracing Impermanence: Finding Joy in the Moment** Life is a series of fleeting moments, each one precious and unique in its own right. "I know you are gonna leave me, but let me enjoy the time until that day comes." It’s a sentiment that captures the bittersweet reality of impermanence—a reminder to cherish the present moment, even as we acknowledge the inevitability of change. In every relationship, there exists an implicit understanding that one day, the bonds we hold dear will be tested by the passage of time. People come into our lives, leaving indelible imprints on our hearts, only to drift away as the currents of life carry them on their journey. It’s a painful truth to confront, yet it’s also a poignant reminder of the beauty and fragility of human connections. But amidst the uncertainty of what tomorrow may bring, there’s an opportunity to find joy in the here and now—to savor the moments of laughter, companionship, and love that we share with others. It’s a conscious choice to embrace each moment with gratitude and appreciation, knowing that it is fleeting and precious beyond measure. Moreover, the acknowledgment of impermanence can serve as a catalyst for deeper connection and authenticity in our relationships. When we recognize that our time together is limited, we are inspired to show up fully, to express our love and appreciation unabashedly, and to create memories that will sustain us long after our paths diverge. It’s also a reminder to cultivate a sense of resilience and inner strength—to hold space for the inevitable waves of grief and loss that accompany the departure of loved ones, while also finding solace in the knowledge that our capacity for love and connection transcends the boundaries of time and space. So, to anyone who finds themselves navigating the complexities of impermanence in their relationships, know that you are not alone. Embrace each moment with an open heart and a willingness to love fully, knowing that the beauty of life lies not in its permanence, but in its ever-changing, ever-evolving nature. #love #hurt #alone #sad #moments

This swimming pool was built on top of the Market Square Tower apartment complex and is called the tallest pool in Texas. It stretches 10 feet (3 meters) out from the building, with a section made of 8-inch (20 cm) thick plexiglass, so swimmers can see the city 500 feet (150 meters) below. It is held up by two concrete cantilevers, one on each side. The tower and pool were finished in November 2016 and were designed by Jackson and Ryan Architects. When a sommelier rotates a wine glass, the rotational forces help keep the wine inside the glass due to a combination of centrifugal force and the shape of the glass. the rotational motion helps to stabilize the wine within the glass due to centrifugal force, the inward curve of the glass, smoother fluid dynamics, and surface tension. This combination of factors makes it less likely for the wine to spill out when the glass is rotated properly. Share this reel with your boyfriends,male friends,dads,brothers,husbands..! 😅 In my practice, I come regularly across males who wet their hair every day with water, without using a shampoo! STOP 🛑 Please don’t do this as plain water is not enough to cleanse your scalp of oil, dirt etc. And it may make your hair DRIER, BRITTLE and lead to more BREAKAGE/HAIR FALL or can lead to DANDRUFF even (colonisation of Malassezia fungi, which can lead to more hairfall)! 📍Pro Tip- Whenever you’re washing your hair, use a little bit of shampoo always to properly cleanse. Yes, it’s okay to use shampoo daily, but make sure it’s gentle/sulphate-free like (Sebamed Everyday Shampoo, Mildly everyday shampoo, Triclenz shampoo..)😊 P.S.- ideal frequency of hair wash is at least 2-3 times a week. Dogs' paws are unique, and these tools can lead to discomfort and even bleeding. The solution is simple: opt for a Dog Nail Grinder, specifically designed for your furry companion. It's a gentle and safe way to keep their nails in check. Remarkably, some dogs even find it enjoyable! You sent an attachment.
Maharashtra has recorded 91 cases of the new FLiRT COVID-19 variants, which also accounts for more than a third of cases in the US. However, there is no cause for worry as of now, a top expert said on Sunday. The new set of variants dubbed FLiRT, majorly includes KP.1.1, and KP.2 strains. These are named based on the technical names for their mutations, one of which includes the letters "F" and "L", and another of which includes the letters "R" and "T". Genome sequencing of March and April showed that Maharashtra has 91 cases of KP.2 — Pune (51), Thane (20), Amravati (7) Aurangabad (7), Solapur (2), Ahmednagar (1), Nashik (1), Latur (1), and Sangli (1). "What we see now, is the result of genome sequencing of the last two months, that is March and April. So, there is no cause of concern immediately as out of the 91 cases, not a single death, hospitalisation, or severe disease has been reported," infectious disease expert Dr Ishwar Gilada, told IANS. "Even the test positivity rate is around 1%," he added. Dr Rajesh Karyakarte, Maharashtra’s genome sequencing coordinator, said that KP.2 has become the predominant COVID-19 strain in the state. However, there hasn’t been a corresponding increase in hospitalisations or severe cases, The Times of India reported. FLiRT variants come from the lineage of the highly transmissible and immune system-evading Omicron. First identified globally in January, KP.2 is a descendant of Omicron’s JN.1. According to the data from the US Centers for Disease Control and Prevention, KP.2 accounted for about one in four or 25% of new sequenced cases in the country in the last weeks of April. Similar to previous variants, the symptoms typically include a sore throat, runny nose, congestion, tiredness, fever (with or without chills), headache, muscle pain, and sometimes loss of taste or smell. . . . #TheTatva #TtavaNdews #India #Maharashtra #COronavirus #COVID19 #Pandemic #ENdemic #Vaccine #Flirt #Spread #Virus #US #Aurangabad #Nashik #Pune #Thane #Mumbai #Record

Listen! Here's some interesting facts about the exam NEET :- NEET is a national-level entrance examination conducted by the National Testing Agency (NTA) for admission to undergraduate medical and dental courses in government and private medical colleges in India. NEET was introduced in 2013 to streamline the medical entrance exams and reduce the burden on students appearing for multiple exams conducted by different states and institutions. The exam pattern of NEET includes multiple-choice questions (MCQs) from subjects like Physics, Chemistry, and Biology (Botany and Zoology). It also has a negative marking scheme for incorrect answers. NEET replaced the All India Pre-Medical Test (AIPMT) and all other individual state-level medical entrance exams to ensure a standardized process for medical admissions across the country. NEET is considered one of the toughest entrance exams in India due to the high level of competition and the vast syllabus that students need to cover. DID YOU KNOW THIS BEFORE?

Oo dear love❤️ In the quiet moments of dawn, When the world is soft and still, I see your beauty, my love, In ways that time can't steal. Your eyes, deep like the night sky, Hold secrets and dreams untold. Long lashes like whispers of the wind, Brush gently, tender and bold. Your messy hair, a wild embrace, Each strand a tale of grace. In your soft, protective arms, I find my safest place. Your caring heart, so gentle, Beats with a love so true. In your shy, sweet smile, My heart finds its view. Oh, my love, you are beautiful, In ways the world may not see. Follow @wander.licious for more travel inspo! How much of this is placebo and how much is real? Weird things that happen on the equator in Ecuador 🇪🇨 Did you know? Loads of weird things happen on the actual equator line, and we’ve just arrived in Ecuador and I HAVE to check it out before we go to the Galápagos Islands. So we arrived on the equator line where the GPS is 0.0, and the first thing they told us its 50 times easier to balance an egg on the equator, so we obviously had a little competition between Mike and I. I’m not gonna lie it was still pretty hard, I was trying for what felt like AGES but if you complete it, you DO get a certificate and lets be honest, I was determined to get it. BUT in the end, it took just under 2 minutes which I thought was not bad. In comes Mike and yeah you can could this, 3, 2, 1. 7 seconds, the jammy bastard 😂 Then they made us do a whole bunch of balance tests because your balance is apparently great on the equator, something to do with how the world is spinning ??? IDK Apparently you’re also physically WEAKER ON the equator line and again, they did the test, and yeah, it seems like she could push us around using just 2 fingers on the actual equator line? BUT I am honestly not convinced if this was the placebo effect. And last but not least, ITS TRUE! the water goes STRAIGHT DOWN the drain on the equator, and in the northern hemisphere the water swirls anti clockwise and in the southern hemisphere it spins down the drain clockwise! Time flies...⏳⌛ . Do you know that theory that says every past time was better? After ageing you get convinced it's true. There are two main reasons, I guess. First, your actual pain always feels stronger, and second, you always forget about bad things that occurred in the past. . The problem is when you're in those 7-8 years of PhD... Everything is magnified... Hopefully you can send your PhD as soon as possible. No need to always be a candidate for anything...
